#<BL1-Style Rarity>

    #<Description>

        By Aaron0000

        Completely overhauls the rarity system.

        Features;

        Each rarity now has three shades indicating loot quality (lighter, medium, darker). Weapon and Item parts will affect the rarity to varying degrees (generally speaking, the better the part (excluding grips), the more it affects rarity.)

        Rarity order is White, Green, Blue, Purple, E-Tech, Gemstone (Unofficial Community Patch), E-Tech Gemstones (for use with the Gemstone E-Techs mod), Uniques (Color is Pre-Sequel's oxygen canister rarity color), Moxxi (optional), Ancient relic rarity, Legendary, Seraph, Pearlescent.

        Override options - Overwrite the rarity of any item with either Unique, Legendary, Seraph, or Pearlescent. Meaning you can get almost any modded weapon/item to be the appropriate rarity without worrying about issues cropping up (unless it mods "BaseRarity" instead of "rarity"). Be sure to load this mod after all of the mods you use that mod weapons/items for the overrides to work properly.

        Easy to adjust the colors - Just look in the "Rarity Breakdown" for clues on what colors what thing.

        Options for mint money and "Moxxi" rarity items (Pulled from Koby's Rarity Color Fix. Thanks Koby.)

    #</Description>

    #<Code>

        #<Rarity Colors>

            #<Rarity Options><MUT>

                #<Standard>
